 Both added 51 runs in six overs of the power play but most of these runs came off the bat of Khwaja
 watasan ne bhi mustafijur par do chauke maare lekin is tej gendbaaj ke over main bhaagyashaalee rahe jab mohammad mithun unka kaich lapakane main naakaam rahe
 Watson hit a six on left-arm spinner Sakalen Sajib but was run out trying to take two runs off the welcome home ball
 unhone 15 gend kaa saamana karte hue do chauke or ek chakka maaraa
 Khawaja completed his first half-century off 37 balls with fours on the welcome
 captain steven smith (14) ne sazib par chakka jadaa lekin agle over main mustafijur ne unhen bold kar diya
 David Warner completed the hundred of the team's runs in the 13th over with fours and sixes off successive balls of Mahmudullah
 al amin ne haalanki agle over main khwaja ko bold karke australia ko teesraa jhatka diya
 Australia needed 38 runs to win in the last six overs
 warner saaqib kii phultas ko waapas unke haathon main khel gaye
 He scored 17 runs off nine balls
 maxwell ne sazib par teen chaukon ke saath gend or ran ke bich ke antar ko kam kiya
 Mustafizur, however, sent Mitchell Marsh (06) to the pavilion in the next over
 maxwell ne mustafijur par do chakke jadkar team ko lakshya ke kareeb pahunchaaya
 Shakib stumps Maxwell at the hands of Mushfiqur, while John Hastings (03) also gets the pavilion but James Faulkner (five not out) hits Sajib to give Australia victory
 shabbir ne jon hastings par do chauke jade lekin watasan kii atirikt oochaal leti gend par mid on par james foconor ko kaich de baithe
 Opener Mohammad Mithun (23) and Saqib Al Hasan (33) tried to build the innings by adding 37 runs for the third wicket
 saaqib ne watasan par chauke ke saath khaataa kholaa jabaki mithun ne mishael marsh par chaukaa or chakka jadaa
 Shakib welcomed Glenn Maxwell with fours and sixes off consecutive balls but Mithun managed to give Watson an easy catch at midwicket off the second ball of leg-spinner Adam Jampa
 chauthaa match khel rahe jampa kaa yah pehla tii-20 antarrashtriya wicket he
 In the same over, Mitchell Marsh caught a welcome home catch
 swaagat (13) ne jampa ke agle over main lagaataar gendon par chakka or chaukaa maaraa lekin agali gend par pagabaadha ho gaye
 Mahmudullah opened the account with fours and sixes on consecutive balls from Hastings while Saqib completed the century of the team's runs in the 15th over with fours on Faulkner
 tippaniyan Jampa gave Bangladesh a fifth blow when the leg-spinner took the outside edge of Saqib's bat into the hands of Colter Neil standing at short third man
 saaqib ne 25 gend kii apni pari main teen chauke or ek chakka maaraa
 Mahmudullah then took the front and hit two fours on Faulkner and Watson
 mushafikur ne bhi in donon par chauke maare
 Mahmudullah also hit two consecutive fours in the final over of the innings on Colter Neil but missed the half-century by one run

 britain main bhartiya mul ke ek bujurg sikh ke saath sharmnaak harakat kaa vakya saamne aayaa he
 In the town of Coventry, a young woman brutally beat up an 80-year-old Sikh
 yah ladki ek luteraa giroh kii sadsy bataai ja rahi he
 The elderly were on their way to City Center Street, when this girl rained on them
 usne unhen bhaddi gaaliyaan deen, laaten maarin or dhakka dekar jameen par gira diya
 When the elderly fell to the ground, this woman spit on their mouth and went away
 is khinchataan main bujurg sikh kii pagadi khul gai
 But the attacker was in bad luck, a person passing by, made a video of the entire incident and shared it on Facebook
 police ab sargarmi se hamalavar mahila kii talash kar rahi he
 According to the police, it could also be a hate-driven attack
 pakade jane par mahila ko paanch saal jail main bitaane pad sakate hai
 It appears in the video that the woman approaches the elder and starts attacking him
 is dauraan teen purush saathi bhi vahiin maujuud hai
 After the robbers leave, a passerby hands the turban back to the elderly
 hamale main bujurg kii naak or aankh par chot lagi he

 Kidney stones are a common problem
 ureen main kai rasinic tatv maujuud hote hai
 Uric acid, phosphorus, calcium and oxalic acid
 yahi saare rasinic tatv stone banane ke liye uttaradaayi hote hai

 kidney main stone ho jane kii vajah se pet main har vakt dard bana rahata he

 haalanki iske upachaar ke liye kai tarah kii davaaiyaan bazaar main uplabdh hai or oparation se bhi iskaa ilaaj sambhav he lekin aap in gharelu upayon ko apanaakar bhikidney ke stone se raahat paa sakate hai

 tarboojamagnesium, phosphates, carbonate or calcium se bane kidney stone ke ilaaj ke liye tarbooz ek bahut acha or kargar upaay he

 potacium ureen main acid level ko mentin rakhane main madad karata he

 ise kidney beans ke naam se bhi janaa jaataa he

 New system of appointment of judges in High Court and Supreme Court During the hearing of the constitutional validity of NJAC, the Central Government once again questioned the Collegium system in the Supreme Court

 baad main hoicourt ke mukhya nyaayadhish ne ritair hone par bataaya tha ki unke virodh ke kaaran sijeai ne unhen supreme court main pramot nahin hone diya

 mukul rohtagi ne kaha ki colegium pranali ke mul nau jajon ke faisle main sijeai ko sarvocch bana diya jabaki samvidhan ke anuchhed 124 main yah kahin nahin hai
 He said that in this decision only control over appointments was considered independence of the judiciary, whereas the framers of the constitution did not even think so
 vahiin supreme court ke paanch jajon ko nyaaypalika kii aazaadee kaa pratik bana diya gaya
 Why five are the only three judges in this because they decide by majority
 kya yah nyaayik swatantraaa he
 Are the other 27 judges of the Supreme Court and the Chief Justice of all the High Courts under these three judges
 tippaniyan The Attorney said that the government appoints constitutional posts like CAG (auditor General), Lok Sabha Secretary General and Chief Election Commissioner, while these institutions are not at all under the government
 inhen bhi jajon kii tarah sansad main mahabhiyog ke jariye hi pad se hataaya ja saktaa he
 The Election Commission conducts fair elections across the country while the CAG conducts a rigorous review of the government's actions

 The people of Uttar Pradesh are happy with the development work of Prime Minister Modi, the people of Uttar Pradesh are supporting the decision like demonetisation, which has started the decisive fight against corruption and black money
 congress evam sapa par nishaanaa sadhate hue unhone aarope lagaaya ki aise log jo chunaav kii ghoshnaa hone ke thik pehle tak subah-shaam ek duusare ko koste the, ek duusare ko rajya kii badahaali ke liye jimmedaar tehraate the, vahiin log aaj ek ho gaye hai
 These parties have become so scared by the atmosphere of development and trust that their decades-old rivalry is being forgotten
 kendriya mantri ne kaha ki hakeekat yah he ki in partiyon ko apni jameen khisakati dikh rahi he
 Somebody's bicycle is punctured, some puncture wants to hold the handle of the bicycle and cross its sinking boat
 nakvi ne logon se apil kii ki ve loktantr ke mahaparv chunaav main 'sushasan or vikaas ke kaaravaan' kaa hissaa bane
 Give a mandate to the BJP
 yah desh, pradesh, samaaj sabhi ke liye acha hoga
 Describing the achievements of the central government, Naqvi said that the Day Dayal Upadhyaya Gram Jyoti Yojana has brought electricity to nearly 11 thousand villages submerged in darkness even after nearly seven decades of independence, not only at home but in the lives of millions of families living in these villages Has also been illuminated
 unhone kaha ki pradhanmantri ujjwala yojana ke tahat desh main pichley ek varsh main 1
 More than 5 crore gas connections have been given for free
 kisaanon kii aamadani ko doguna karne ke liye kai kadam uthaaye gaye hai
 Schemes like Beti Bachao Beti Padhao, Sukanya Samriddhi Yojana are dedicated to women power
 pradhanmantri kaushal vikaas yojana main lakhon yuvaaon ko rojgarparak training di gai he taaki 'har haath ko kaam' dene ke hamaare lakshya ko puraa kiya ja sake
 The comments nakvi ne aarope lagaaya ki uttar pradesh main centre sarkaar kii vibhinn yojanaon or centre dwaara vikaas hetu bheje ja rahe dhan kaa durupyog ho rahaa he
 He said that to make Uttar Pradesh a model state, it is necessary to bring a BJP government
 (is khabar ko enditivi team ne sampadit nahin kiya he
 It is published directly from the Syndicate feed
 ) He alleged that while on one hand the Congress has become a 'benami property of unscrupulous', with a 'two-let' board at its door, Samajwadi Party has become the 'tenant' of this benami property
 nakvi ne aarope lagaaya ki basapa 'bahubaliyon or beyimaanon kaa baseraa' ban gai he
 The Union Minister said that the BJP will form the government in Uttar Pradesh with a strong majority by 'dividing the forces of the unscrupulous'
 'samaveshi vikaas or vishwaas' par yakeen rakhane vaali bhaajapa hi samaaj ke sabhi virgo kii tarakkee kii guarantee he
 Naqvi said that villages, poor, farmers, weaker sections, Dalits, minorities, youth and women are the focal point of every welfare scheme and program of the government headed by the Prime Minister Narendra Modi
 hamaara sankalp 'har garib kii ankhon main khushi or jindagi main khushhaali' laana he
 He said that the goal of Prime Minister Modi is to bring the light of development to the last person of the society
 congress, sapa, basapa jaise dalon par tushtikaran kii raajnneeti karne kaa aarope lagaate hue nakvi ne kaha ki 'tushtikaran ke bina shashaktikaran' kaise kiya jaataa he, yah bhaajapa kii centre sarkaar ne kar dikhaaya he

 isamen 1

 Prime Minister Narendra Modi will inaugurate the first 'khelo India School Games' program at the Indira Gandhi Stadium in the national capital today
 'khelo india' kaarykram kaa uddeshy jamini str par khel samskruti ko punerjeevit karnaa he

 a high level committee will identify the youth sports talent and they will be given financial assistance of five lakh rupees per year for eight years
 'khelo india' kaa aayojan 31 janvari se 8 farvari tak rashtriya rajdhani main kiya jayega

 ) Controversy over cartoons published by the Shiv Sena mouthpiece Saamna over the silent procession of the Maratha Kranti Morcha is increasing
 maharashtra vidhaan sabha main vipaksh ke netaa radhakrishna vikhe patil ne mangalvaar shaam ko pune main is silsile main shivasena pramukh uddhav thakare or sampadak sanjay raut par maamla darj kiye jane kii maang kii he
 Talking to reporters in Pune, Radhakrishna Vikhe Patil said that Kishiv Sena's mouthpiece Saamana has not only mocked the agitators who were peacefully agitating, but the lakhs of women who joined this front and the martyrs have also been insulted
 unhone kaha ki shivasena pramukh or saamana ke sampadak par jald se jald exiaar darj kii jaani chahie

 vipaksh ke netaa radhakrishna vikhe patil ne kaha ke is cartoon ke kaaran jo apmaan mahilaon or shaheedon kaa hua he uske liye shivasena pramukh komaharashtraki janata se maafi maangani chahie

 odisha ke balasore loksabhaa seat par matdaan 29 april ko he

 is loksabhaa seat par congress ne navajyoti patnayak ko tikat diya he
 Five independent candidates are also contesting from here
 yahaan se kul 12 ummidavaar maidan main hai
 Srikanth Jena, who was in Congress on this seat, had a strong hold in the area, but this time he is different from Congress
 lihaaja is seat kii ladaai romaanchak ho gai he
 Political background Balasore is a Lok Sabha seat in Odisha where BJP has won the election thrice
 is seat par biju janata dal ne 2014 main pehali baar jeet hasil kii
 In the initial Lok Sabha elections after independence, the Congress ruled here
 1951, 57 or 62 kaa chunaav congress ne jeeta
 In 1967 the CPI opened its account on this seat and Samarendra Kundu emerged victorious
 1971 main congress ne yahaan phir vaapasi kii
 After the anti-indira wave in 1977, the Congress lost from here and Samarendra Kundu won the elections once again
 1980 or 84 main congress kaa paracham is seat par phir fahraaya
 Samarendra Kundu won elections on the Janata Dal ticket in the 1989 election
 1991 or 96 main yah seat congress ke khate main gai
 In the era of atal-advani, this seat played lotus
 1998, 99 or 2004 main yahaan bijepi ke tikat par kharbela swen chunaav jite
 In 2009, the Congress benefited from the break-up in the alliance between the BJD and the BJP and Srikanth Jena won from this seat on the Congress ticket
 haalanki 2014 main yahaan se bijedy ke rabindra kumaar jena vijayi hue
 Recently Srikanth Jena has been removed from the primary membership of the party by Congress President Rahul Gandhi for anti-party activities
 haalanki jena pichley saal disambar main hi pradesh congress cameti se istipha de chuke the
 After his removal from the party, Srikanth Jena accused Odisha Pradesh Congress Committee President Niranjan Patnaik of being involved in the mining scam
 shrikant jena ne congress adhyaksh rahul gandhi par bhi hamalaa kiya tha or kaha tha ki agar vah rahul gandhi kii pole kholenge to vah munh dikhaane laayak nahin rah jaaenge
 The 2014 mandate saw a major reshuffle in this seat in the 2014 Lok Sabha elections
 2009 main chunaav jitkar kendriya mantri banane vaale congress ke netaa rahe shrikant jena ko is seat par haar kaa munh dekhnaa padaa
 He came third in this election
 biju janata dal ke rabindra kumaar jena 4 lakh 33 hajaar 768 vot laakar pehle number par rahe
 He won the election with 1 lakh 41 thousand 825 votes
 bijepi ke pratap chandra saarangi 2 lakh 91 hajaar 943 vot laakar duusare number par rahe
 The former Union Minister received 2 lakh 77 thousand 517 votes
 sipiai ke prashanth kumaar mishra ko bhi lagbhag 15 hajaar vot mili
